# Work Orders & Crafting Contracts Pack 1

Repeatable contracts to create economy sinks + routing.

## WO-GLI-0001
- **Profession:** Tailoring (Journeyman)
- **Region:** Glimmerdeep_Mire
- **Request:** brew 5 units
- **Turn-in NPC:** NPC-GLI-0176
- **Payment:** recipe chance

## WO-SAL-0002
